Recent News of the Lishi Painting Exhibition

The success of the Lishi Calligraphy and Painting Exhibition has been widely reported in various newspapers. In recent days, the "Times," "French Shanghai Daily," "English Continental Daily," and other newspapers have all published favorable reviews. The number of visitors has reached over 50,000. As the weather turned cooler today, the number of visitors was even more crowded. Among them were the President of Jiaotong University, Li Zhaohuan, the newly appointed Minister to Sweden and Norway, Wang Jingqi, and his daughter. Despite being about to embark on a new mission abroad, they still remembered culture and art and made a special trip to the exhibition to admire the famous works from various provinces. They praised Zhang Shiqi's "Spring in Jiangnan" for its magical brushwork and elegant coloring, calling it unprecedented and unparalleled. They also praised Hu Zhaobin's "Clear Breeze and Bright Moon" for its ingenious depiction of animals, novel composition, and antique coloring, truly worthy of being a contemporary master. Due to lack of time, they were unable to visit and comment on all the other famous works and left in a hurry. The exhibits at the exhibition have been updated.

Two Robbers Apprehended in Lujiazui, Pudong

One Handgun Confiscated

In the areas of Yangjiazhai and Haixing Road in Lujiazui, Pudong, five or six robbery cases have occurred in the past few months. The perpetrators have not yet been apprehended. Zhang Haigen, the leader of the second team of the Yangjing District Self-Defense Corps, was instructing his subordinates to rigorously pursue the matter. On the evening before last, at around 6:00 PM, he received a tip that a group of bandits was meeting in the Sanwanchang area. He immediately dispatched squad leader Zhu Paixiang and section chief Yang Zhongfu to lead officers to investigate. Two robbers, Zhen Mei from Ningbo and Xu A'gen from Haizhou, were arrested on the spot. A fake handgun was found on Xu. The witnesses were taken into custody. After questioning by Zhang, the two confessed that the ringleader was named Wang Axiang, a Ningbo native. They and Wang Axiang, along with the fugitives A'miao, A'fa, and Sanmei, committed several robberies in Pudong. The first time was on April 1st of this year, when they robbed Lu A'da's house in Chunhui Lane, Tieban Bridge, and stole over 90 yuan. The second time was on April 13th, when they robbed the Dafeng Cigarette and Paper Store on Lujiazui Road and stole over 90 yuan. The third time was on May 10th, when they robbed Chen Guihua's house at No. 55, Haixing Road, and stole over 70 yuan. The fourth time was on the 24th of last month, when they robbed the Yin family's house at No. 9, Peideli, Land Temple Road, Yangjiazhai, and stole an amount they had forgotten. Tonight, Wang Axiang called the two of them to meet in front of the Wanguo Cinema in Hongkou to rob a cigarette and paper store next to a laundry shop on Gongping Road, but they were caught instead. They also said that Wang Axiang lived next to the Yangjia Bridge in Yangjiazhai. The squad leader then ordered Zhu Paixiang and others to continue to capture Wang Axiang. One bullet and several pawn tickets were found on Wang. Wang confessed that he had been sentenced to five years in prison for committing a crime in the Public Concession. In addition to the fake handgun, he also had a real handgun, which he borrowed from Laipi and which was later borrowed by A'mao Baobao, who committed a crime in the French Concession and was imprisoned. The squad leader verified the confession and summoned the victims to identify the three men without error. He ordered that the three men, the fake handgun, and the bullet be sent to the Pudong branch office for interrogation yesterday afternoon.

Suicide Pact in Wu Gong Hotel

Yesterday afternoon at around 6:00 PM, the tea server at room 429 of the Wu Gong Hotel at No. 151 Fujian Road discovered that a guest named Wang Tiansheng, an Anhui native, 27 years old, and a woman had taken poison. They were sent to Renji Hospital for treatment, but the treatment was ineffective, and they both died. This has already been reported. Upon investigation by the Laozha Public Security Bureau, only a suicide note was found, addressed to the hotel. It stated that they had been staying at the hotel for four days, had not missed any room fees, and that they were a married couple who had been running a store in Hangzhou. Business had been poor recently, and they were experiencing extreme financial difficulties, making life unbearable, so they resorted to this. An empty opium box and two bodies were found. The police transported them to the Filial Piety Road Coroner's Office. Yesterday, Prosecutor Tang was dispatched by the First Special Court to examine the bodies and confirm that the bodies were indeed the deceased Wang Tiansheng, male, and a female surnamed Wang. They had died from opium poisoning. There were no family members of the deceased, so the bodies were handed over to the Pushan Villa for collection.

Zhang Junhong Dies After Being Hit by Car: Autopsy Held at Court Yesterday

Zhang Junhong, a Sanbei native, 42 years old, residing at No. 79, Tongle Lane, Huasheng Road, Pudong, had a pregnant wife, Ms. Mu, who was suffering from diarrhea. Yesterday afternoon at around 1:00 PM, the couple was riding in a rickshaw pulled by Wang Fuchang, intending to seek treatment from a doctor on Nanjing Road and Shilu Road. As they were traveling east on Dongxi Huade Road near Huaji Road, a cargo truck No. 16611 suddenly sped up from behind. The truck driver attempted to overtake Zhang's rickshaw, and the rear wheels hit the rickshaw, causing it to overturn. Zhang Junhong suffered severe head injuries, while Zhang's wife and rickshaw puller Wang Fuchang suffered minor injuries to their hands and feet. Upon hearing the report, the police arrived and summoned an ambulance to the scene. Zhang was rushed to Tongren Hospital, but the treatment was ineffective. He died at 9:35 PM that night. The Huishan Police Station conducted an investigation and transported the body to the Filial Piety Road Coroner's Office. Yesterday morning, Prosecutor Tang was dispatched by the First Special District Court to examine the body. The police reported the previous situation and stated that they had ordered the truck driver to be present this morning for questioning, but he had not arrived. According to the investigation, the incident was caused by slippery roads due to rain yesterday. Wang Fuchang stated that he pulled rickshaws for a living. Yesterday, he was pulling rickshaw along the side of the road when the car came up from behind and hit the rickshaw. He could not see it coming. Zhang Mu stated that she was 34 years old. After falling from the rickshaw yesterday, she suffered minor injuries to her hands and feet, and her abdomen was in pain all night and she vomited blood. Her family situation was extremely difficult, and she requested that the truck driver compensate for everything. After obtaining the statements, Tang ordered the police to continue the investigation and declared that the deceased Zhang Junhong, male, had died as a result of being hit by truck No. 16621. His body was released to his wife, Zhang Mu, after she signed a statement.

Hua Dafan and Gu Xuelin's Marriage Dispute in Court

Hua Dafan (also known as Da Wei), the owner of the Yuchengfeng Fruit Factory on Yongji Lane, North Zhejiang Road, was previously sued by Gu Xuelin, a 33-year-old woman from Suzhou, in the First Special District Court for seduction and abandonment. The grounds for the lawsuit stated that Gu was originally married to a man named Chen and lived in Suzhou. In August of the previous year, she met Hua Dafan through an introduction at a dinner party. She was seduced into an affair and divorced her husband. She then began living with Hua. On January 18th of the previous year, a contract was signed at the law office of Zhang Shijie, stating that the wedding would be held within one year, or Hua would have to pay 50,000 yuan in damages. Later, Hua reneged on his promise and abandoned her, so she filed the lawsuit. The case was heard and concluded by the Special Court, which ruled that Hua Dafan was innocent. It is now learned that Hua has hired a lawyer and filed a petition with the Civil Court of the First Special District, requesting to dissolve the marriage contract with Gu Xuelin. Yesterday morning, Judge Mo Runhua summoned the parties to the Sixth Civil Court for questioning. The plaintiff, Hua Dafan, did not appear and was represented by his lawyer, Wang Shou'an, who explained the case. The defendant, Gu Xuelin, also arrived in court with her lawyer, Gu Yongquan, and filed a counterclaim, requesting that the contract signed at Zhang Shijie's law office be declared valid and seeking damages of 50,000 yuan. The court stated that since the defendant had filed a counterclaim, she must pay court fees, and the case was adjourned for further review.

Gao Jimin Establishes Minli Sanatorium

Mr. Gao Jimin, a physician currently serving as a medical officer on the Shanghai Municipal Self-Defense Committee, is a highly respected physician in Shanghai. He has served as a physician at the Chinese Red Cross Society's Municipal Hospital and as the director of the Pingmin Sanatorium. To serve society and promote the health of citizens, he has invested a large sum of money to establish the Minli Sanatorium at No. 692 Hankou Road in this city and has set up a preparatory office at No. 702 Hankou Road to actively carry out the preparations. The sanatorium has a well-organized structure and perfect equipment. Many specialized physicians with extensive knowledge have been hired to handle internal, external, and other departments. The various treatment machines used are all the latest models imported from Europe and the United States. The arrangement of the sickrooms is all for the patients' benefit. They are not only clean but also strive for low fees, in line with the economic ability of the average citizen. The interior decoration has been completed, and service will begin by the end of this month. The opening date will be in the first ten days of next month.

Two Fires in West Shanghai

Grass Shed Destroyed: Yesterday morning at around 1:00 AM, a fire broke out at the grass shed of Weng A'er, a Dongtai native, at No. 5 Qian Hu Jiahong, west of the Tongren Bridge in Xujiahui Town, West Shanghai. The flames quickly engulfed the area and were uncontrollable. By the time the fire trucks arrived, the fire had been extinguished. Two grass sheds were destroyed. The police station in charge summoned Weng A'er to the police station for questioning.

Burned Mosquito Net: Wang, 37 years old, a Yangzhou native, residing at No. 160 Zhoujia Bridge, West Shanghai, accidentally started a fire at around 7:00 PM the night before, which burned his mosquito net. Neighbors heard the news and called the Caojiadu Fire Brigade, which dispatched a truck to extinguish the fire. Wang had already extinguished the fire with water, fortunately preventing a major disaster. The police officers on duty arrested Wang and brought him to the police station for investigation.

Inferior Oil Sold Under False Pretenses Seized

The Huali Grocery Store on Waima Road in Wusong used to sell flour, kerosene, and miscellaneous grains, and its business was quite good. Recently, the owner, Yu Zhengming, became greedy and purchased inferior oil. Because he could not sell it all at once, he bought a large number of old kerosene cans from companies such as Asia and Mei Fu, poured in the inferior oil, and sold it on the market. After a period of time, the Asia Company learned of this and sent Chief Inspector Fan and Mei Fu Inspector Ge to Wusong to investigate. Posing as customers, they found more than fifty cans of inferior oil in the store. The Wusong Chamber of Commerce intervened to mediate the matter. The inferior oil was confiscated and burned, and Yu Zhengming issued a letter of repentance and apologized in the newspaper.

Car Registration Stolen

Zhou A'chang, a 34-year-old Yangzhou native, residing at No. 12 Wuzhou Road, Hongkou, owned a car for transportation. The Chinese registration number of the car was 4156, and it was displayed on the car. Recently, the car registration was stolen. It was later discovered that the registration number was on a car dispatched by the Songhu Automobile Company at the Wenzaobang in Wusong. Zhou reported the information to the North Station Branch Bureau, which went to Wusong Public Security Bureau to investigate. The registration number was found on a piece of black paper. The driver, Wang A'rong, a Binbo native, was suspected. After being questioned at the police station, he confessed to the theft. He was then transferred to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for investigation.

Yu Jinkun Struck by Lightning

Yu Jinkun, 44 years old, a native of Jiangwan, residing at No. 22 Baiyangzhai, Jiangwan, made a living by selling vegetables. At 6:30 PM the day before yesterday, he carried three baskets of vegetables on his shoulders to Jiangwan Town to sell them overnight. As he was walking near Shenjiazhai, it suddenly started to rain heavily with thunder and lightning. Yu had nowhere to hide. At that moment, lightning struck the ground, killing Yu beside the road. His body was black. When the rain stopped, passersby saw it and ran to inform his family. Only his old mother and an adopted daughter were at home. They rushed to the scene and cried loudly. The police station in charge ordered Li Baoxian, the local security officer of the 26th Tu, to report to the local court for an autopsy.

Central Bank Inspection Report

Central Bank Exchange Note Issuance Reserve 296th Inspection Report states: In accordance with Article 13 of the Central Bank Law, this Committee is responsible for inspecting the number of exchange notes issued by the Bank and the reserve fund. On August 15th of the 25th year of the Republic of China, the 296th inspection was held at the Bank's Issuance Bureau. The inspection results are reported as follows: (A) The total amount of exchange notes issued is 30,420,317 silver dollars, including 27,192,456 silver dollar notes and 3,228,2861 subsidiary currency notes. The total amount of exchange note reserves is 30,420,317 silver dollars, including 20,375,7817 silver dollars in cash reserve. This cash reserve includes 10,725,8747.29 yuan stored in the Bank's issuance general and branch treasury and various branches, and 9,649,9069.71 yuan stored in peer institutions. The guarantee reserve is equivalent to 10,044,5500 silver dollars. (B) The total amount of customs gold exchange notes issued is 400,9630.07 yuan. The total amount of customs gold exchange note reserves is 400,9630.07 yuan. This reserve includes 7,926.290 ounces of pure gold, valued at 51.68 Customs Gold dollars for a total of 400,9630.07 yuan. In accordance with Article 22 of the Central Bank Law, the cash reserve must be at least 60%, with the remainder guaranteed by legal guarantees. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60% and the guarantee reserve is within 40%, which is in compliance with the law. This report is specially made. August 18th, 25th year of the Republic of China, Central Bank Supervisory Board Chairman Li Fusun, Supervisors Xie Mengjun, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Jilong.

Shanghai's Film Industry

— Compiled by China Credit

(A General Overview of Shanghai's Industry and Commerce, Part 34)

(3) Business Methods of Film Companies

(2) The United China Film Company - This company was formed by the merger of companies such as Grand China, Lily, Minxin, and Shanghai. It initially had a capital of 400,000 yuan, with Sir Robert Ho Tung and Lo Weng-kan as directors, and Lo Ming-yau as general manager. It was officially established in October 1930. In the past, it adopted a branch factory system, with a total of seven factories set up one after another. Factories 1, 2, 4, and 6 were located in Shanghai, Factory 3 was located in Hong Kong, Factory 5 was located in Beiping, and Factory 7 was located in Sichuan. Later, Factory 4 was destroyed in the Songhu Battle, Factory 5 was closed due to the September 18th Incident, and Factory 7 was closed due to the Sichuan Rebellion. As a result, on the one hand, the capital was increased to 1 million yuan, and on the other hand, the factory system was changed to a unit system based on standards. Shanghai Factories 1, 2, 6, and 3 were changed to factories 1, 2, and 3, and Hong Kong Factory 3 was changed to the Hong Kong Film Studio. The Shanghai Company, originally Factory 4, separated from Lianhua and was independently reorganized into the Shanghai Sound Film Company. After Luo returned from studying in the United States, the company was reorganized into a collective factory system. On January 1, 1935, a centralized plan was announced, and on April 1, all factories in Shanghai were concentrated in Xujiahui. The original site of Factory 1 was expanded, and the internal organization was rectified. The company's products were of excellent subject matter, able to cater to the psychology of the general youth, but due to insufficient working capital, production was slow. There are currently more than 200 employees and actors, with monthly expenses of about 15,000 yuan. A list of the company's output over the years is listed below:

The company's previous films, except for "Wild Grass and Flowers" and "Milky Way Double Stars," were dubbed by Yi Moling. Now that it has purchased sound recording equipment, it has already made two sound films, "Waves Wash the Sand" and "Song of a Loving Mother."

(3) Tianyi Film Company - This company is jointly operated by the Shao Zuiweng brothers. It was initially a partnership, but now it has been reorganized into a company. It was established in 1920 in the Republic era. It has a branch office in Nanyang, managing the company's and other companies' products. The company's address is located at 232 Ganshidong Road. Its output is quite rapid. In 1931, it purchased Movietone sound recording equipment and produced sound films. In addition to producing its own films, it also shoots films for small companies, such as the Ancient Company's "Si Lang Visits His Mother" and the Southern Company's "Platinum Dragon." In the past few years, it has produced more than 80 silent films and more than 30 sound films, making it the company with the most output in Shanghai. The company has a branch factory in Hong Kong. Since last year, due to the difficulty of establishing a foothold in Shanghai, it has focused its efforts on developing the Hong Kong factory, producing Cantonese sound films that cater to the psychology of overseas Chinese in Nanyang. The scope of the Shanghai general factory has been reduced compared to before. Recently, the New Era Company was closed down, and all the actors who played "Mr. Wang" have rejoined Tianyi. It is rumored that they are currently engaged in the production of a sequel to "Mr. Wang." The company currently has more than 100 employees, with monthly expenses of about 10,000 yuan. (To be continued)

Shenbao National Goods Special Edition

Words of Contribution

Interview with Housewives

— Yang An

The family is centered on the housewife, and the biggest customers of national goods are families, and the power to purchase them lies in the hands of the housewife. If housewives love to use national goods, the promotion of national goods will be as smooth as fire starting to burn or water flowing downhill. Therefore, promoting and advocating national goods should start with the family. It is absolutely necessary to start from the housewife's perspective.

We have interviewed housewives from middle-class and upper-class families to inquire about their opinions on using national goods. Most of them are happy to purchase national goods, believing that Chinese people should use Chinese goods, which is a matter of course and without hesitation. However, after using them, they often feel that national goods still have the following shortcomings, and they hope to find ways to improve them: (1) The products lack standardization. Often, the same item has one form the last time, and the next time it has already changed its appearance, and even the color, texture, and effectiveness vary from time to time. (2) The decoration is still not elaborate enough. The packaging and boxing lack research. (3) The value has not been able to strive for low prices, mostly because the cost is not easy to reduce at one time. (4) Often, when users need a certain product, it cannot be supplied, and other types or secondary brands are used to muddle through. (5) They only like to imitate others and fail to preserve the inherent beauty of China. This is in regard to the factory side. There are also opinions on national goods stores or companies: (1) The clerks lack a spirit of service. Purchasing goods often takes a long time, which is annoying. (2) National goods are not fully stocked, and prices are inconsistent. (3) They fail to guide customers in detail, explaining the nature and effectiveness of certain goods and comparing them with foreign goods. These are the unsatisfactory points in using national goods, which were said by more than one hundred housewives and can be used as a reference for manufacturers and sellers. Now the Shanghai National Goods Movement United Association has sent people to interview housewives to persuade them to use national goods. This kind of very meaningful and valuable work is indeed a fundamental strategy for promoting national goods. I sincerely hope that it will be realized as soon as possible. Therefore, I state what I have seen in order to promote its success.

A Few Words on National Cigarette Paper

— Meng Zhao

What is most regrettable about the current national goods business is that although the products of factories are purely national goods, the raw materials are not national goods, or the raw materials contain imported goods. In this regard, the authorities in charge of national goods factories should earnestly take responsibility, think deeply and anxiously about replacing them with national goods, and resolutely reform. In case there are no national goods to replace them, they should study and contribute to the reproduction of them by Chinese people. Now, the Jiaxing Minfeng Paper Mill can utilize this point to manufacture national cigarette paper and invite the Shanghai press to visit. The cigarette paper has already been used by the Nanyang Brothers Tobacco Company as the first adopter. It cannot be said that our country's national goods business is gradually progressing - good news has arrived, and we are all deeply delighted! The consumption of cigarettes in our country is really alarming! Taking the example of ten cigarettes per person per day, and taking Shanghai as an example, with one million smokers, it requires ten million cigarettes, averaging one cent of national currency per cigarette, costing 100,000 yuan a day! If we combine the national statistics, isn't it alarming? And the percentage of money spent on "paper," turned into ashes, should not be small. The huge leakage is heartbreaking! Therefore, the Minfeng factory's national cigarette paper is especially valuable! I sincerely hope that all national cigarette companies will adopt it unanimously. Because of the national cigarette paper, I think of the newsprint for large leaks, and I hope that in the near future, I will also get a happy news that there is a "national product"!

The National Goods Movement in Extraordinary Times

— Ying

It has been several years since the Chinese people realized that the influx of foreign goods into the market would cut off China's economic lifeline, and began to launch the national goods movement. However, if we review the past and carefully examine the achievements of the national goods movement in recent years, then what I say will make you feel disappointed. If you don't believe me, we only need to see that the number of excess imports in recent years has still not fallen, and we can conclude that the effect of advocating national goods is minimal! In fact, in this extraordinary period, the Chinese people can no longer perfunctorily deal with the national goods movement, making it only in name and increasing the country's difficulties. Therefore, every citizen, especially in extraordinary times, should understand the importance of advocating national goods and intensify the work of the national goods movement.

The effective way to promote national goods is definitely not to achieve results by talking empty words. The most important point at present is that everyone can lead by example. Local authorities should first implement the use of national goods, so that the civil servants below will also use national goods; school teachers should first use national goods, so that students will not use foreign goods: the head of a family, if he can use national goods himself, the children will dislike using foreign goods. The words say to promote national goods, but the food and utensils at home are mostly foreign goods; elementary school teachers tell students the importance of the national goods movement, but he himself wears a suit; this kind of promotion of national goods, it can be said that the effect is equal to zero, so the promotion of national goods must be based on leading by example!

At the same time, in this extraordinary period, factories can no longer produce shoddy goods, because the low quality of goods in the market will definitely not be able to compete with foreign goods. We have good national goods, so that the Chinese people can use national goods and slowly squeeze foreign goods out of the markets everywhere; therefore, every factory should pay special attention to its own products, carefully study them, and strive for excellence, so that the quality of the goods is excellent, and then can compete with foreign goods. Therefore, national goods factories can no longer ignore their responsibilities, and should improve the quality of their products and improve the manufacturing methods in order to cope with this extraordinary period.

That is, workers, in this extraordinary period, in addition to improving the items they produce, should also do their best to increase the rate of production, because the increase in the rate of production can reduce the cost of national goods, and the cost is lower. Competing with foreign goods, it is naturally easier to obtain profits. Therefore, in this extraordinary period, every worker should understand the importance of the mission he bears, do his best to promote the progress and increase of production, and strive to produce for the society and the country. Of course, it is the greatest duty of workers to cope with this extraordinary period.

The current smuggling problem in North China is so serious that this problem, directly and indirectly, can cause the national goods industry to die and intensify our economic crisis in extraordinary times. In fact, we only need to think carefully, and the so-called smuggling problem is not without a way to deal with it. So what method should be used to deal with it? As long as everyone is of one mind and one virtue and does not use foreign goods, the smuggled goods, in order to evade taxes, can be cheaper in price, but no matter how cheap they are, we will not buy them, then even if there is smuggling of foreign goods, it will not hurt me. Therefore, the determination not to use foreign goods is an effective way to deal with the smuggling problem, where the people of the country can implement the refusal to use foreign goods.

The Impending Disappearance of Jiangyin Native Cloth

— Jin Rentong

At a time when we are calling for resisting foreign goods and promoting national goods, there is a kind of genuine national goods that is about to fall into decline. This is a matter of great concern.

Those who know the place of Jiangyin all think it is an important national defense town. I don't know that Jiangyin also has a special product of native cloth, which is a kind of farmer's sideline. Jiangyin native cloth is woven from pure national goods yarn. There are roughly two kinds: Du cloth is thicker and suitable for making shirts and pants in cold weather. Factory cloth is thinner and can be used as underclothes in spring and summer, or as outer robes and long shirts. They all have the advantage of being durable. In the past, when the country was closed off, in addition to solving the clothing problem of the people in Jiangyin County; it could also be sold to various places to assist economic circulation. Since foreign goods rushed into the market, due to the growth of users' aesthetic concepts. And the factory's adherence to old methods and failure to make improvements. Not only has the sales volume in foreign ports sharply decreased, but the position of native cloth in the county has gradually shaken. Moreover, the factory is tempted by the low prices of foreign raw materials. Make the native cloth popular in the market, and it will only exist in name.

Resisting foreign goods is the principle of saving the national industry and commerce. And promoting national goods is a prerequisite for resisting foreign goods. National goods should be promoted, how can we allow them to disappear? Then this pure national goods, so that the Jiangyin native cloth that is not worthy of the name, I hope that some experts will study and improve it. I also hope that the general patriotic compatriots will promote and use it. Because it still has the advantage of being durable.

The Difficulties of the National Goods Industry

— Ba Ling

At present, the most serious problem that the national goods industry feels is the alarming North China smuggling problem. According to a survey by the Greater Shanghai Evening Post reporter, since the North China smuggling problem occurred, the industrial and commercial circles have been seriously affected by the following items:

1. In the past, Shanghai was the hub for the import of silk stockings, but the situation has changed drastically today. The servants of the ships traveling to and from Shanghai and Hong Kong are smuggling large quantities of silk stockings to Shanghai for sale. The profits are higher than their salaries, because the import tax on Shanghai silk stockings is 100%. When these ship servants disembark in Shanghai, they hide the silk stockings in their clothes, and no one can find them when they land.

2. A certain paper merchant talked: At present, there is no trade in North China. The reason why the Shanghai market has not been affected is that a large number of papers are too heavy to be smuggled easily, but it is only a matter of time. Sooner or later, it will be affected.

3. A certain general merchandise manager said: The impact on our business has two types: The first is the Tianjin branch. In the past, the general merchandise stores in Tianjin purchased goods from Shanghai. Since the start of smuggling, all business has been completely gone. Second, some of the goods sold by us have actually been smuggled to various places, and the business future is really unimaginable.

4. …

According to the above, we can know that since the occurrence of the smuggling problem, our industrial and commercial circles have been seriously affected. At a time when the national goods movement has achieved some success. Unfortunately, the North China smuggling problem occurred. This is not only a problem that the North China industrial and commercial circles should urgently pay attention to, but also a major difficulty that cannot be ignored in the entire national goods movement.

The China General Federation of Industry and Commerce said in its report to the Ministry of Industry requesting to stop smuggling in North China: "Smuggling in North China is alarming to the entire country's industry and commerce! The harm to our country's production industry is so deep and great that it is difficult to maintain it now that all industries are depressed. How can we bear this major blow? … Not only the national goods market, but also the influence of our country's tariff revenue, is harmful to the extreme?…" These few words are what we want to say but have not said. In order to protect the nascent national goods industry, the government must use lightning speed to stop the major North China smuggling problem. We must know that this is a difficulty for the national goods industry. If the industrial and commercial circles and the government authorities do not cooperate to solve the North China smuggling problem, the future of national goods is really not optimistic.

Rober Cup Doubles Preliminary Round - China Suffers a Miserable Defeat to the United States - Score 3-0, Close Scores, US Obtains Right to Quarterfinals - Another Group Portugal Wins Over Japan, Set for Quarterfinals on Saturday at the French Chamber of Commerce

International Tennis Rober Cup Doubles Preliminary Round - China vs. United States. Yesterday afternoon, the match took place at the Kang Ti Club. The Chinese side was represented by He Jialiu and Zhou Guanjun, against the American team of Carson and Squier. He Jialiu served first and won the first game. Carson also served to tie the score at one-to-one. The Chinese side proceeded smoothly and won two more games, leading with a score of three to one. Then, when it was He Jialiu's turn to serve, the Chinese side was in an excellent position. Unexpectedly, after two deuces, they unfortunately lost the game. From then on, misfortune befell them. They repeatedly made mistakes at critical moments, and thus lost the first set with a score of three to six. In the second set, the American side took the first three games, but they were not easily won. He Jialiu bravely and persistently fought, using short volleys and long shots, and won back two games. After five to two, He Jialiu again served to win a sliding game, making it three to five. In the end, it was difficult to recover due to the mismatch between strength and will. They lost the second set with a score of three to six. In the third set, the American side again led with a score of two to zero. The Chinese side calmly responded and reversed the situation to lead with a score of three to one. Then, the American side caught up to tie the score. The Chinese side also won a game with a serve, still leading with a score of four to three. At this time, the two sides were even more closely contested, and it was exceptionally exciting. Unfortunately, they quickly lost three games, and again lost the third set with a score of four to six. As a result, the United States won the right to the quarterfinals with a score of three to zero. It is scheduled to compete with France for the final spot this Saturday (the 22nd). In another preliminary round group, Portugal has already defeated Japan the day before yesterday and is also scheduled to compete with England in the quarterfinals this Saturday. Both groups will be held at the French Chamber of Commerce court, starting at 3:45 PM. Tickets are one yuan. England has the highest hopes for this championship. Although Carson's individual skills are excellent, his partnership with Squier is not as skilled as the British team of De Voe and Pona Victoria.

Record of the First Day - Joint Annual Meeting of Seven Scientific Societies - Jiang Menglin Explains Two Methods of Scientific Research - Chinese Science Society Elects Ren Hongji and Others as Directors - Bing Zhi Talks About Animal Competition and Survival, Detailing Darwin's Theory

(Special Dispatch from Beiping) The 21st Annual Meeting of the Chinese Science Society, the 2nd Annual Meeting of the Mathematical Society, the 5th Annual Meeting of the Physical Society, the 4th Annual Meeting of the Chemical Society, the 3rd Annual Meeting of the Zoological Society, the 4th Annual Meeting of the Botanical Society, and the 3rd Annual Meeting of the Geographical Society have all been under preparation for a long time. These seven scientific societies held a joint annual meeting today (the 17th) at Tsinghua University in the western suburbs of Beiping. The opening ceremony was held in the morning, and the Chinese Science Society held a board meeting and public lectures in the afternoon. Tsinghua University also opened an academic exhibition. Details are recorded as follows:

Grand Opening Ceremony

Members of the seven societies from various places arrived in Beiping separately yesterday. This morning (the 17th) from 8:00 to 10:00 AM, registration continued, with a total of over 400 members arriving. At 10:00 AM, the opening ceremony was held in the auditorium of Tsinghua University. In addition to all the members, guests Wang Lengzhai, Yuan Tongli, Zha Liangzhao, etc., totaling over 600 people, were also present. The chairman of the conference, Jiang Menglin, gave the opening speech, stating that today is the opening day of the joint annual meeting of the seven academic societies. Many members of the societies from other places have come to participate. He would like to briefly express his welcome on behalf of the academic circles of Beiping. There are two ways to research academics: one is for individuals to bury themselves in research in libraries or laboratories, and the other is to gather many people together to discuss together. Thus, the organization of academic societies began. Today is the day for members of the societies to begin gathering. He hopes that they can make considerable contributions to the country, society, and culture. In China, whether in social sciences or natural sciences, there have been organizations of academic societies in recent years, separately and collectively discussing a problem, and there have been significant achievements. The beginning of science is due to questions. Of course, the questions in the universe are not just the falling of an apple. Many unresolved or undiscovered problems await our resolution. It is expected that from this moment of budding, great fruits will be born. At this moment, he would like to take this opportunity to bless the health and eternal progress of the seven scientific societies and all colleagues. Then, Mei Yiqi gave a welcoming speech on behalf of the academic circles of Ping City, followed by a speech by Wang Lengzhai on behalf of the mayor of Beiping. He stated that it is an honor to attend the opening of the joint annual meeting of the seven academic societies today. Mayor Qin originally planned to come in person, but due to temporary matters, he was afraid that he would not be able to arrive on time, so he specifically asked him to represent him. At the same time, Mayor Qin also represented the 1.5 million citizens of Beiping to welcome everyone and expressed a few hopes: (1) Science should be applied to society and should be expanded nationwide. Although the seven societies now have members in various places, it is still hoped that they will continue to expand and become national organizations. (2) Foreigners often study a certain subject from their youth to their old age. This spirit of persistence should be our model, so that our research work can also be long-term and continuous. (3) Because science is not developed in our country, many great raw materials must be sold to foreigners for manufacturing and then shipped back to China, absorbing capital. Those of you who study various sciences should have the same feeling. He hopes that they will work tirelessly and strive for progress. Then, member representative Ren Hongjun gave a reply speech. At 12:00 noon, the photo session was dismissed.

Parties Hosted by Various Parties

After the meeting, Tsinghua University hosted a lunch for all members and guests in the first dining hall. The seats were prepared by Jiei Ying Western food. Over 600 people used their knives and forks and toasted each other. Although there was no scene of glittering lights and wine, this grand occasion was also rare in the academic world. During the meal, the host Mei Yiqi also gave a modest speech, saying that he was ashamed that the school's hospitality was not adequate for those who had come from afar. Before lunch was over, Chairman Song expressed his regret for not being able to attend due to official business. He has now scheduled to prepare a small feast at Huai Ren Tang in Zhongnanhai at 6:00 PM the day after tomorrow, hoping that everyone will honor him with their presence. Qin Dechun also expressed at the same time that in order to save time for everyone's official business, the arrangement for him to host at Zhongshan Hall is planned to be changed to the same time as Chairman Song's banquet, so as to enhance the joy. At 2:00 PM, everyone dispersed happily.

Chinese Science Society Board Meeting

At 2:00 PM, the Chinese Science Society held a board meeting in the Tongfang Department of Tsinghua. Ren Hongjun chaired the meeting and said that he was very pleased that members from various places had gathered together for today's meeting. The existence of the Science Society today is due to everyone's efforts. Yang Xiaoshu's report stated that the progress of the society's affairs in the past two years is as follows: (1) Promoting advanced research: The Nanjing Biological Research Institute is working hard on research. (2) Popularizing scientific knowledge: Expanding science libraries in Nanjing and Shanghai. (3) Publishing two regular publications: Science Monthly, with monthly sales of 3,000 copies, and Science Pictorial (bi-monthly), with monthly sales of 15,000 copies. The society is carrying out its work according to the above two principles. The society has a total of 11 staff members in Shanghai and 31 in Nanjing. The number of members has increased significantly this year, with 99 new members, bringing the total to 2,500. The Alumni Association has long been established in ten places: Nanjing, Shanghai, Beiping, Suzhou, Hangzhou, Kaifeng, Wuzhou, Guangzhou, Chongqing, and Qingdao. This year, Alumni Associations have been newly established in Chengdu and Tianjin. In terms of donations, Jin Shuchu donated shellfish books worth 50,000 yuan and another US$300. Ye Shanding donated 2,000 medical books. Chen Zongnan donated 50 yuan for Science Pictorial. Two scientific experts were invited: the physiologist Karlsen and the mathematician Hadamard. Xiang Bingzhi reported on the situation of the Biological Research Institute. There is considerable exchange of academic research with the United Kingdom, the United States, Germany, France, Japan, and Russia in international relations. The Accounting Editor reported one after another. Finally, the staff was elected, and the results are as follows: (1) Seven directors were re-elected: Ren Hongjun, Hu Xianqi, Zhou Ren, Li Siguang, Wang Jin, Sun Hongfen, and Yan Jici were elected. (2) Two auditors were elected: He Dekui and Chen Qinghua. (3) Three election committee members were elected: Wu Xianwen, Dong Shijin, and Yuan Hanqing. The meeting adjourned at 4:00 PM.

The Question of Animal Competition and Survival

At 4:10 PM in the afternoon, a public lecture was held in the Biology Museum. Animal expert Bing Zhi gave a lecture on the survival of animals. In addition to members of the Zoological Society, there were Tsinghua biology teachers and students and guests, totaling over 400 people. First, President Hu Jingfu gave an introduction. Then, Bing took the stage to give a lecture, stating that there are nearly one million species of animals, which is more than the number of species of plants. The results of zoologists' research have found over 900,000 species so far. Insects account for more than two-thirds. There are more insects than stars. Because of the suitability and unsuitability of animals to the environment, a distinction between breeding and elimination has evolved. Because animal reproduction and breeding are geometric progressions, the result of competition and conflict is harm and extinction, which can be seen anywhere. The issue of animal competition and survival can be divided into two parts: (1) Animals' resistance to the environment: (1) Resistance to climate. During the Ice Age, it was suddenly extremely cold. Animals could not resist this extremely cold climate and froze to death. Glyptodon, which was originally a Tank Armediils elephant, Mastodon, and Grart Slotk were all large animals and froze to death because they could not resist the climate. Other animals with thick fur, such as camels and rhinoceroses, can resist the climate and do not freeze to death. (2) The relationship with food. Reptiles and dinosaurs eat many plants. Once the plants change, herbivores, reptiles, and large salamanders all starve to death, while ordinary reptiles and toothed animals survive. Because small animals have less food intake, they can survive. (3) The impact of disease. Large animals have small parasitic animals on their bodies. If small animals are sick, large animals also die from the disease. When I was a student, I saw Eurosta (flies) with parasites on their bodies called Eurotonea in the first year. In the second year, I didn't see these flies anymore, which shows the impact of disease. (2) Animals' own or conspecific or heterospecific killings: (1) Food. Food is limited in an area. Animals compete with each other, and conspecifics or heterospecifics kill each other. The weak starve to death or are killed. The fact that cats eat mice is the easiest to see. According to zoologists, ruminants such as cattle and horses store food in their stomachs because they compete with other animals for food. After the other animals leave, they ruminate and spit it out before eating it again. This is the origin of ancient ruminants. (2) Space. Animals compete for territory. The strong kill the weak, or the weak escape. England originally had many black rats. Later, Norwegian gray rats invaded England. A few years later, the black rats became extinct, and England was occupied by Norwegian rats. This is the result of competing for territory. (3) Mates. When a male sparrow courts a female sparrow, two male sparrows must fight. As a result, the weak fail and die, and the strong snatch the female sparrow. This result of competing for mates is enough to cause one side to become extinct. He hopes that the young people present will not kill each other because of this issue. (The whole place roared with laughter.) American Horndacc specializes in sexual fighting. The weak have no wives and will never have offspring, resulting in many extinctions. Humans are also animals. Because they can prevent natural and man-made disasters, they can resist the environment. Cultural aggression and military aggression between countries are also related to the survival competition. Darwin's theory of evolution is at least partially reliable. Human brains are developed, so they can conquer everything. The lecture ended at 5:40, and the whole audience applauded and dispersed.

Tsinghua Academic Exhibition

Tsinghua University held an academic exhibition today (the 17th) to welcome the seven scientific societies. All the exhibitions were presented in the Biology Museum. 1. Agricultural Products Exhibition: Over a thousand kinds of agricultural products are displayed, including those with research results: (1) Mole crickets are most harmful to sorghum and corn. The department has invented white mail stone, which can cure mole cricket nodules. (2) Milk is concentrated on the tree and can cure aphids. (3) Grape golden bugs are treated with Paris green. (4) Maize earworms are easily known to have earworms, and 80% are affected. They are being treated with cold temperature methods and are currently under research. 2. Animal life wave, the following tests listed by Zhao Yibing Wang Zhi: (1) Bottom temperature stimulates meat, electrical current stimulates muscles, measurement of free radicals concentration. 3. Wood Exhibition: Biology students collected over 50 kinds of wood, including new records: red paper birch, white paper birch. 4. Fish Pond is divided into two parts: (1) Goldfish genetics. Department Head Chen Sunxi has carefully studied and discovered many hereditary properties. (2) Studying animal sociology, animal psychology, animal social organization, animal cooperation, solving the principles of human society, using ants as test products, because ants have cooperation like human society (Jin)

Municipal Education Bureau Orders Adoption of - The Maze Intelligence Test

For the purpose of recruiting kindergarten and lower grade students, the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued an order stating that the summer vacation of all schools is about to end and school will start soon, and new students are to be recruited. All kindergarten and elementary school lower grade freshmen should be divided into classes according to their intelligence level, so that teaching will be most effective in the future. The Bureau previously compiled this test in response to the needs of various schools, and it has been completed, that is, the raw materials of the American Bode Maze Test were adopted and revised. The results are quite suitable for the application of grading kindergarten and elementary school lower grade students in our country, and all testing methods, procedures, materials, and scoring methods are described in detail in the "Maze Intelligence Test Report Special Issue" in the eighth issue of the second volume of Great Shanghai Education. Now, in order to facilitate enrollment in various schools, an order is hereby issued for compliance, and the schools are ordered to adopt the test to grade kindergarten and elementary school lower grade students, and submit the test results for verification and future revision. This is an order.

Five Academic Societies Donate Funds for Zhejiang University Scholarship: Fund Set at 3,000 Yuan for "Engineering Scholarship"

The Chinese Institute of Engineers, the Chinese Society of Electrical Engineers, the Chinese Chemical Industry Society, the Chinese Society of Chemical Engineering, and the Chinese Society of Automation Engineers, five academic societies, held a joint conference at the National Zhejiang University in Hangzhou from March 20th to 23rd of this year. To commemorate the event and the founding of the Chinese Society of Mechanical Engineers and the Chinese Society of Civil Engineers during the annual conference, a special allocation of 3,000 yuan was made from the joint annual conference to establish a fund named the "Engineering Scholarship." The annual interest earned will be used as scholarships specifically donated to the Departments of Civil Engineering, Mechanical Engineering, Electrical Engineering, and Chemical Engineering of the College of Engineering at National Zhejiang University. Each year, one student with the best academic performance in the third year from two of the aforementioned four departments will receive the scholarship, and the following year, students from the remaining two departments will receive it. A special management committee will be established, consisting of the President of Zhejiang University, the Dean of the College of Engineering, and the Chairman of the Joint Annual Conference and President of the Chinese Institute of Engineers, who will serve as committee members. The President of Zhejiang University will be designated as the chairman of the committee. The announcement date is set for July each year. Students who receive the Engineering Scholarship will also be granted a one-year exemption from tuition and dormitory fees by Zhejiang University (for their fourth year) as a form of encouragement. Furthermore, scholarship recipients will be exempt from membership fees when joining any relevant engineering academic societies, which is indeed a significant initiative.

Junior High School Geography Textbook Map: Tan Lian's Latest Masterpiece

In recent years, maps published in the market have been improving with each passing day, showing considerable progress. However, finding one that complements the textbook and is suitable for the curriculum is rare. The Junior High School Geography Textbook Map, recently published by the Zhonghua Cartographic Society and compiled by Tan Lian, has changed various previous publishing habits. Not only are the place names adopted based on the junior high school geography textbooks published by various publishers, but the name of each map is also distributed according to the latest revised geography curriculum standards, such as the central region, southern region, and other local maps; the national defense map for national defense; the Zhongshan Railway Plan map for the Zhongshan Plan; and the Zhongshan Improved Harbor and River Management Plan map. These are all indispensable maps for junior high school geography. Instead of using the same old descriptions after the map, the latest statistical tables of various industries and transportation are used for reference, which can supplement the shortcomings of textbooks and is a special feature. Moreover, the county names in the map are selectively drawn, and the place names not adopted in the textbooks are omitted except for those that are particularly important. As a result, the characters are sparse and particularly clear, and the colors are bright and very eye-catching. The railway, highway, aviation, and other lines are drawn according to the latest traffic routes. It can be called the best educational map without shame, and the price is also cheap. The current special price is seven jiao, distributed by Qinfen Bookstore at 277 Sima Road, Shanghai.

New Unpolished Rice Floods In, Prices Drop Two to Three Cents

Yesterday's customer rice market was quite active, but prices fluctuated, not uniformly soaring despite the active trading. Generally, old stocks of various customer rices and machine-polished rice saw price increases of one to two cents due to lively trading on the local street and customer demand. However, unpolished rice prices dropped by two to three cents due to the influx of new goods and active arrivals from all routes. Producers in producing areas also advocated selling off goods at market prices, with many telegrams requesting sales. Brokers competed to sell on their behalf, causing market prices to fall. However, after the price drop, unpolished rice sales were still good. It is estimated that 5,000 bags of Shashi unpolished rice were opened, while machine-polished rice included 1,770 bags of Gan rice, 3,160 bags of Xiang rice, and 840 bags of Wen Tai rice. These were distributed from the local street to the interior, Xiamen, Shantou, Beiyang, Ningbo, and other places.

Investigation: Economic Research Department of the Central Bank Releases Production Index for April

Due to seasonal factors, the production volume of major industries in January, February, and March of this year showed a slight decrease, but April saw significant improvement compared to the spring, increasing by about 10%. May saw a slight decline, also due to seasonal influences. The Central Bank's recently released production index is listed in the table below. This index began compilation last year, and the methodology was revised this year. The calculation method is detailed in the Central Bank Monthly, Volume 5, Number 6, and the Central Bank English Quarterly, Volume 2, Number 2. Readers can review these. China Production Index (Monthly Average for 1933-1935 = 100)

Soybean Cake Sales in Shantou Market Very Active, Foreign Firms Expand Sesame Seed Holdings, New Soybeans Trend Flat

Foreign firms have been holding sesame seeds for the past two days. Although foreign firms sent telegrams at $12.78 the day before yesterday, there has been no response from abroad as of yesterday, so no transactions have been made. Few people in the market are selling because there is still little certainty about the harvest this year. Only general dealers are active in the market, so asking prices are rising daily, with some considering selling at $13, leading to a lack of transactions between the two sides. Except for soybeans from Chengmen, which see some activity from small-scale millers, and the fact that stocks are accumulating, causing prices to continue to fall by 5 to 6 cents, the rest are trending flat. Sales are also sluggish. It is estimated that 3 to 4 thousand bags of various beans were opened, and the future is not optimistic. Soybean cake sales in Shantou are increasingly active, with prices rising by 1 to 2 cents, and 17 to 18 thousand pieces of various factory brands were sold.

Dried Goods: New Honey Dates Still Arriving in Small Quantities

Since the new honey dates came on the market, the harvest in the producing areas has been poor this year, and the cost of raw dates is relatively high, so the quantity of goods arriving from Jiaxing, Lanxi, and other places has been small in recent days. The market is gradually trending flat. In previous years, Lanxi products were superior to Jiaxing goods, but the current goods are inferior. Yesterday's market price for bald dates was $35, the same price as Jiaxing goods. Top-grade dates are priced higher as usual. The market is temporarily stable. If more goods arrive in later batches, there may be hope for a loosening.

Oil Market: Tung Oil Plummets, Hankow Telegram Reports Foreign Firms Dropping to 54 Yuan

Due to the large quantities of tung oil being transported from Guangxi Province to Hunan Province for sale, the price of tung oil has plummeted recently. Half a month ago, foreign firms in the Macau market were still at around 75 yuan per picul, but in just ten days, it has fallen to 60 yuan. The situation remains depressed. Unexpectedly, last night, this port received a telegram from Hankow stating that the price has plummeted to 54 yuan, a catastrophic decline. However, because the fall has been so rapid, any movement is sensitive. If there is a slight turnaround, the change will also be rapid.

Random Thoughts

Tidbits

— (Ye Zhongxun)

Patience and motivation, like loyalty, have the power to move mountains and overturn seas. When there is still hope for a matter, do not give up, but also do not hope beyond reason. This indicates that your ambition has exceeded the bounds." Pana tells us that within the realm of possibility, hope is the companion of strength, the mother of success. Because those who have resolute hope do not harbor any desires for unexpected things. Behind hope follows courage, so Catherine said: "I beg you to summon courage, this brave spirit can eliminate all disasters." Napoleon said: "Energy of character is the foundation of true hope, a strong heart always holds hope… even when all is lost, it can still maintain itself! Its own perfection and value hope awakens courage, and despair is the last of all evils, it is the abandonment of welfare! A complete retreat from the battlefield of life." As long as our hope has not been extinguished, courage will always accompany us, because hope is backed by courage.

Melon Eaters and Melon Growers

— Zhou Xian

Watermelon, with its refreshing fragrance and sweetness, is said by medical experts to have considerable nutritional value for the human body. Therefore, in recent years, although soda, ice cream, fresh orange juice, shaved ice, and other cold drinks have occupied a large position among summer cold drinks, watermelon is still selling well without obstruction. In every household, watermelons are still piled up in corners, and the streets are filled with the shouts of watermelon vendors. It is truly worthy to say "Long live watermelon."

Urban dwellers, because of the high price of melons, often envy the rural people who grow watermelons. And some people often reveal in their conversations, "Rural people are really happy, they can pick a watermelon from the field to eat, how enjoyable!" However, "Though fields stretch to the four seas, the farmer still starves," these words can also be used to describe watermelon growers. The author grew up in a rural village and knows a thing or two about the lives of farmers. Although the distance from planting seedlings to harvesting watermelons is shorter than growing grains, if the price of melons is high, then eating one melon is like eating the profit of one melon. If the price of melons is low, then the farmer spends capital and labor, and the proceeds from selling are not even enough to pay rent, causing them to worry to the point of tears in their eyes, unable to eat with relish, unable to sleep soundly, so where would they have the mood to eat watermelon? Therefore, in rural villages, there are often fields full of ripe melons, but the watermelon growers are still drinking water from the ditches to quench their thirst.

The biggest enemies of watermelons in the fields are badgers, foxes, hedgehogs and the like. These animals often sneak into the melon fields at night to steal melons. Therefore, watermelon growers usually set up tents next to the melon fields to guard them. Once they see such animals appear, they gather neighbors to help watch and drive them away or arrest them. At the same time, watermelon thieves are also very active. After guarding so carefully and cautiously until the melons are ripe, they pick them and sell them to melon vendors to recover the capital and labor costs spent on growing the melons. If the melons ripen too early, before the weather has become scorching hot, then this season's hard work is only left to a sigh. Because when the weather is cool, it is difficult to get a good price. If the melons ripen during the height of summer, clearing the stomach and making one feel refreshed, then the watermelon grower will have a slight smile on their face, which is even darker than the skin of pickled ginger. But during the day, when planting watermelons, they suffer from the summer heat, and at night, when guarding, they suffer from the cold. By the time summer passes and autumn arrives, the melon eaters have already grown tired of eating watermelons, and the watermelon growers are found at the entrance of the village. In addition to compasses, sundials are also their unique business. Sundials sell best in Hunan.

Melon eaters are indeed lucky, and melon growers are indeed pitiable. However, if melon eaters pity the watermelon growers and do not eat watermelons, then that would be terrible, as it would be cutting off the watermelon growers' source of livelihood. Therefore, every year when watermelons come on the market, "Should I eat watermelons? The watermelon growers are too pitiable." "Should I not eat watermelons? How will the watermelon growers live?" These two contradictory but reasonably valid viewpoints are always circling in my mind.

Natural Refrigerator

— Rong Yu

In times when science was not very developed, eating popsicles in June would really be considered an earth-shattering and impossible thing. But now, we have sanitary machine-made ice; we have natural ice stored for freezing in winter; and we have "ice cream" and "shaved ice" produced in connection with ice. In the hot summer, ice is an indispensable thing for every household in the city to cool their hearts and minds.

In the past, when there was no machine-made ice and no way to preserve natural ice, people used well water as a refrigerator. Because well water is deep underground, its temperature is lower than general water. If you have leftover food, you are afraid that it will spoil overnight, so you often hang it in the well. Also, if you cook cold jelly and want it to freeze quickly, you also soak it in well water. In addition, melons and fruits are also soaked in well water to keep them cool. Don't you see that well water in summer is like a refrigerator today? Moreover, at that time, most families did not have tap water. If they lived far from a river, they would almost all dig a well for washing clothes and vegetables, so this natural refrigerator was quite common. When I was young, I relied entirely on this well water for cold food in the summer!

Jiangsu and Zhejiang are low-lying and watery, so digging a well is not a difficult task. Digging two or three feet deep into the ground will produce clear and deep well water. In the past, there were also specialized workers who dug wells, commonly called "hook and bait craftsmen." I am afraid that this industry no longer exists in Shanghai. Well digging took place in hot weather, and the craftsmen had to drink enough white wine and wear a broken cotton-padded jacket when they reached the bottom of the well, which shows the temperature at the bottom of the well. The form of an ordinary well is small at the top and wide at the bottom; from the bottom of the well to the ground, it is built with tiles to prevent the mud from collapsing; the top is a well railing, which is chiseled from stone, in circular, square, and hexagonal shapes. Water is drawn with a wooden bucket, tied with a palm rope. There are also some small techniques for drawing water. Those who are used to it will put the bucket on the surface of the water and shake the rope slightly, and they will get a bucket of clear and deep well water. Those who are not used to it will thump! Thump! Using all their strength, the water is both turbid and the bucket is not full. It is now rare to see such well water in Shanghai, but if you go to the interior, there are quite a few.

Kuang Junyou of Lingui, also known as Han Weiqi, is the wise son of the poet of the Huifeng Pavilion. He has inherited the family's scholarship, is skilled in poetry and calligraphy, and also likes painting. He held a gift to enter the gate of He Shisun and Jiang Yingsheng, and tirelessly practiced painting day and night. The landscapes he creates are simple, sparse and vigorous, sweeping away the habits of coarse expansion and overbearing. In recent times, those who learn to paint mostly fear difficulties and seek ease, painting with rough branches and large leaves, and then boast that they have obtained the Dharma milk of Bada Shanren and Shitao. There are few who can discuss ancient methods. Mr. Kuang relies on his natural talent and also learns from famous teachers, so he can understand the essence of this art. He has extensively viewed the famous works of past masters collected by Wang Xicun and Kang Gengsheng. He has virtually copied all of them, so he can break away from the mundane styles and not specialize in one school. On the other side, it was paired with Liu Jungonglu's running script. Both gentlemen are sons of famous fathers, and those who saw it all said that they were evenly matched. A New Home for the Phoenix

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter Five: Good Fortune Repeatedly Depicted on Green Leaves, Bridal Dress Startlingly Tried On, Tears Wetting the Gauze

After dinner, Menglan seemed to have something urgent to do, and hurriedly ran upstairs. She closed the door, and sat under the lamp in a daze. It seemed that she had found a solution to a problem. She immediately stood up, opened the box, and took out the letter with the poem written by Guoqi to read it again. This gave her an idea. Then, she placed all the drawing tools she used for school drawing assignments on the table. From the book box, she picked out a very good double-ply Xuan paper, cut a piece more than a foot long, and laid it on the table. Then, she sat upright in the chair, facing the blank paper, paying close attention to it for a long time. It was as if someone was sitting under the lamp, discussing something with her. So, after she smiled slightly, she dipped her brush into the paint palette with plenty of color, and in one breath, without stopping, she drew four or five green, long and short orchid leaves on the paper. Then, she used a lighter green to outline a stalk of orchid. Among them, there were two more mature flowers, to which she added a light purple. Below the flower stalk, she applied powder and carefully outlined it with carmine. These few strokes of flowers and plants were truly graceful and charming. She did not think that the painting had too few strokes, and immediately put down the brush. She stood outside the table two or three feet away, held her hands in her arms, and stared at the painting. Suddenly, she frowned slightly, as if she felt a kind of melancholy again. After a long time, she muttered to herself: How should I sign it? After she finished speaking, she completely removed the drawing tools from the table, and then pinned the painting on the wall with drawing tacks. She sat on the chair, leaning sideways, staring at the painting in a daze, while raising one hand to gently support her left cheek. After she had pondered for half an hour, she finally figured out how to sign it. This method of signing, even when it reached Guoqi's hands, Guoqi felt it was very appropriate. This painting reached Guoqi's hands when it was already. Originally, after Guoqi sent the letter, he seemed to have tied a knot in his heart again. The words in the letter might cause someone to become angry and submit the letter to their parents. If the parents saw it, they could tolerate it and let it go. If they did not tolerate it, the trouble would be no small matter. Thinking carefully, it was always his own fault. He should not have used words to provoke a young lady. From now on, no matter how confused he was, he would never write a single word to her again. Respecting others is also respecting oneself. It would be at least thirty years before Chinese men and women reached the level of open communication. It would be too early to use Western customs as a comparison. With this thought, in addition to completely fading the desire to pursue Miss Jiang, he also bore a sense of fear in his heart, feeling that there was a faint fire constantly burning in his heart. Spring in Shanghai

— Jiang Gong

When I lived in Qiantang, I wandered around the lake every day and night, but I never really appreciated the beauty of the West Lake's mountains and waters. Then I traveled to Beijing, and after living there for a long time, I still did not know the beauty of the old capital. Now, I think about it a little, and I quite hate that I wasted the beautiful scenery in front of me. I am afraid that I will inevitably be ridiculed for swallowing scallops whole, and I feel even more ashamed and regretful. This is like sitting opposite a beautiful woman, and completely forgetting the beauty of her eyebrows. After the illusion is shattered and dispersed, there is longing for the beauty. Only then do I realize that her demeanor is perfect, and every detail of her sleeves and skirt is beautiful, but the paradise is so close, and the beauty is hard to obtain again! The ancients said that what we cherish most is the past, and what we neglect the most is the present. How true, how true! Although, in the ten miles of foreign concessions, the scenery is boundless, what is there worth cherishing in the future? We should seize the present and not be negligent! "The green hills are still the customs of Yangzhou, and how many peaks cannot cross the river," here the material civilization is something that the green willow city walls cannot even dream of, but the vulgar and hateful scenery is suspected to be more than doubled than there. This poem can be borrowed to sing about it.

Jiangnan has long been known as a soul-stirring place, and the vulgar saying also uses paradise to describe Suzhou and Hangzhou, but in recent times, Shanghai has taken its place. In the past, Huang Xie and Lord Chunshen were small towns located in remote coastal areas, not scenic areas or places of gentle beauty. After the sea ban was lifted, foreign ships gathered like clouds. As a result, all kinds of undertakings flourished, people from all directions gathered, and it became the only major commercial port in the East. I once read a novel written by an Englishman, which was full of ridicule for the beauties: criticizing them for being vulgar, greedy, and lacking elegant bones; depicting the nouveau riche and the poor snobs, being vulgar, uncultured, mean, and ungrateful. The description was so vivid and the satire so sharp. At that time, I really wanted to give this description to the Shanghai men! Not only is it true of the people, but is it not also true of the place? There is no mountain or water, or beauty of bamboo and stone, not to mention the beautiful gardens and ponds here. What is rare to see is like phoenix feathers. Spring comes and spring goes, the so-called "good times and beautiful scenery, what a waste, whose house is the enjoyment" is like the spring breeze not passing through the Jade Gate Pass. What is revealed to us is only the silent passage of time. I once lamented: living in Shanghai for a long time is like being placed in the desert. There is no human habitation, and even the sound of footsteps is rare. Being isolated from the world, the vitality is exhausted. Not only are the famous gardens of Luoyang and the beautiful flowers of Heyang hard to come by, even more so than the heavenly peaches and the red apricots by the sun, even the wildflowers and the tired flying birds are hardly seen or heard all year round. Even white poplar withered grass, maple leaves and reed catkins are treasured as much as colorful flowers and plump beauties. Ninety years of youthful time have passed quickly, and spring never comes to the world. What can be gained and randomly guessed, and carefully experienced, is a common feeling, a different taste, as if still receiving the gift of the gurgling sound outside the curtains, the spring rain in the small building, and the east wind rain last night. Alas! This is Su Wu's life of lying on ice and snow in the northern border! Ten thousand kinds of worries, loneliness, who to tell, the pain can be imagined. The former Napoleon said that there are no difficult words in the dictionary, and I think there is no spring in the dictionary of Shanghai people!

Special Report

Returning from the Slums

— Ya Fei

Summer is a terrible season when plague ghosts run rampant and diseases are rampant. As long as you are not careful in your daily diet and daily life, you will get sick. Therefore, at this time, those who want to maintain health and reduce danger should first pay attention to cleanliness and hygiene. Whether it is what you eat, use, wear, or how you move and rest, you must be careful at all times to reduce the chance of pain and disease entering.

Especially the poor who are struggling on the poverty line, their lives have no rules, their actions are often abnormal, and they lack hygiene knowledge even more. Therefore, according to newspaper records and statistics from health authorities, the number of deaths each summer is the highest among the poor. Therefore, I often think and hope that hygiene campaigns should be brought to the poor as soon as possible.

Living a very prosperous life in the city, I can be said to be completely ignorant of the lives of those poor people who are excluded from the urban circle. Moreover, if we compare our lives with theirs, then I would suspect that I and they exist in two different worlds.

"How can we make their lives the same as ours?" Yesterday, after returning from an inspection of the slums, I suddenly had such a thought. But in the end, I myself admitted that my consciousness was wrong, because this is fundamentally impossible!

In these places, not to mention living, even if you ask me to stay for an hour or two, it is impossible. But yesterday, for the sake of my duties, I finally inspected there for as long as two hours, and I carefully analyzed every dirty corner.

There, there are no towering foreign buildings, no smooth asphalt roads, and no streamlined motorcycles. Here, there is only a group of poor people who have been forgotten by the people of the metropolis. — A shallow, narrow river surrounds a damp wasteland. Seventy or eighty short thatched cottages are squeezed unevenly on the wasteland. Some women and children are working leisurely or playing in the open space in front of the door or under the eaves of the thatched cottages. As for the structure of these thatched cottages, it is very ridiculous and simple. Many broken pottery jars and broken lead sheets discarded in the garbage heap can be used as their building materials. Some people even drag a broken sampan to the shore and consider it a house. Moreover, most of the thatched cottages are short and small. It really doesn't look like a house, but it looks a bit like a chicken coop or doghouse. There are no windows or back doors. If a fire breaks out, I really have to worry about them.

In the small river, there is only some filthy bottom water left. A foul odor often rises from the bottom of the river and spreads through the air with the wind. The surrounding open space also evaporates the smell of urine and feces, making me feel nauseous and want to vomit. Many mosquitoes and red-headed flies are practicing there without order, as if they were soldiers in a military camp. The water they drink is drawn from the deepest section of the small river, and they wash rice and other things there. The children are all naked, and the women either wear a vest, or a broken and dirty short shirt, or expose their upper body and only wear a bellyband. But they are all as dirty as a mud bodhisattva.

However, when I asked them, I was very surprised. Not only are they content with this kind of life, but they also have not expressed any dissatisfaction with this environment. Therefore, I realized that as long as a person can be content with their own real life, then they can be satisfied with any bad environment. On the contrary, even if they go to paradise, they will feel dissatisfied.

However, I feel that their unhygienic habits must be improved...
